       </a>
       <p class="supplement">
        不同的葡萄品种、风土、酿造工艺能够使葡萄酒展现出截然不同的果香，因此，果香能够在品鉴中为你提供线索。本文就向你介绍葡萄酒中常见的果香以及相对应的葡萄酒种类。

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function Mousemove(id) {
             if (id == "AuthorityScore") {
                 $("#AuthorityScore").className = "curr";
                 $("#AuthoritativeAwards").className = "";
                 $("#AuthorityScoreul").style = "display: block;";
                 $("#AuthoritativeAwardsul").style = "display: none;";
             }
             else {
                 $("#AuthorityScore").className = "";
                 $("#AuthoritativeAwards").className = "curr";
                 $("#AuthorityScoreul").style = "display: none;";
                 $("#AuthoritativeAwardsul").style = "display: block;";
             }
         }

         function getQueryStringByName(name) {
             var result = location.search.match(new RegExp("[\?\&]" + name + "=([^\&]+)", "i"));
             if (result == null || result.length < 1) {
                 return "";
             }
             return result[1];
         }



         var userAgent = navigator.userAgent;

         if (getQueryStringByName("fm") == "" && (
             userAgent.indexOf("Android") >= 0 ||
             userAgent.indexOf("Mobile") >= 0 ||
             userAgent.indexOf("Fennec") >= 0 ||
             userAgent.indexOf("iPhone") >= 0 ||
             userAgent.indexOf("iPad") >= 0 ||
             userAgent.indexOf("Nokia") >= 0
             )) {
             window.location.href = "http://m.wine-world.com";
         }



         ////平台、设备和操作系统
         //var system = {
         //    win: false,
         //    mac: false,
         //    xll: false,
         //    ipad:false
         //};
         // //检测平台
         // var p = navigator.platform;
         // system.win = p.indexOf("Win") == 0;
         // system.mac = p.indexOf("Mac") == 0;
         // system.x11 = (p == "X11") || (p.indexOf("Linux") == 0);
         // system.ipad = (navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) != null)?true:false;
         // //跳转语句，如果是手机访问就自动跳转到wap.baidu.com页面
         // if (system.win || system.mac || system.xll||system.ipad) {
         //     window.location.href = "http://m.wine-world.com";
         // }

         //产区大区
         $(".reg-gj li").mouseover(function () {
             $(".reg-gj li").removeClass("curr");
             $(this).addClass("curr");             
             $(".reglist").css("display", "none");
             var ids = $(this).attr("dataname");            
             $("#" + ids).css("display", "block");            
         });

         //酒庄大全
         $("#showToWinery span").mouseover(function () {
             var ids = $(this).attr("dataname");
             if (ids == "winery11") {
                 return;
             }
             $("#showToWinery span").removeClass("curr");
             $(this).addClass("curr");

             $("#winery1One").css("display", "none");
             $("#winery2One").css("display", "none");
             $("#winery3One").css("display", "none");
             $("#winery4One").css("display", "none");
             $("#winery5One").css("display", "none");
             $("#winery6One").css("display", "none");
             $("#winery7One").css("display", "none");
             $("#winery8One").css("display", "none");
             $("#winery9One").css("display", "none");
             $("#winery10One").css("display", "none");
             //  $(".winery-tl").css("display", "none");
             $(".winery-bl").css("display", "none");

             //var ids = $(this).attr("dataname");

             var thisIdsOne = ids + "One";
             var thisIdsTwo = ids + "Two";

             $("#" + thisIdsOne).css("display", "block");
             $("#" + thisIdsTwo).css("display", "block");

             if (ids == "winery11") {
                 window.location.href = 'http://www.wine-world.com/winery';
             }
         });

         $("#showToWinery span").click(function() {
             var ids = $(this).attr("dataname");
             if (ids == "winery11") {
                 window.location.href = 'http://www.wine-world.com/winery';
